Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageHoliday by Atria
URLhttps://holidayseniorliving.com/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1238
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1238, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 439. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 2. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 133

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 131 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 111

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 16 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 11 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 98 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 33

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 31 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 27

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 16 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 10 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 13 (Text has insufficient contrast)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 24

Issue reports in this category:

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:
